info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:2.7
posted:Posted September 9, 2023
msg:We booked 2 rooms. Because the schedule for one of them was uncertain, we booked it for one night. When we checked in, we told the front desk that we could extend our stay and go directly to apply. However, the next day, the front desk told us that the room type was fully occupied and we had to extend our stay. Changing rooms... Because of the epidemic in the past two years, I was used to changing disposable bedding and disinfecting some items by myself when staying in hotels. Changing rooms midway meant doing it all over again and packing up scattered daily necessities. After expressing that it was very troublesome, the front desk still Stick to this one plan, and if communication fails, the only option is to change rooms. Looking at Ctrip's rave reviews about our hotel's free room upgrade, I don't understand why we can't also upgrade subsequent guests staying in the same room type as me? I can move without any fuss and everyone will be happy. The irony is that after I finished moving, the original house type was available on the platform again. Obviously, I had already avoided the summer season when I made the reservation.
I prepaid the room fee and deposit for the next two days of the new room. I asked the front desk for the new room card and gave it to me. They were all on the same floor. After packing up the original room, I moved directly there. The front desk refused directly. I had to check out and check the room first. In the future, give me a new room card... which means I have to go downstairs with my luggage and go through a set of procedures before checking in again. It's really embarrassing. You have collected all the room fee deposits later. What are you worried about? In your Territory, I'm afraid you can cut off the power to the room at any time if I don't restore the room card. After another difficult communication, the front desk reluctantly agreed and said nervously that they would call us after the move was completed and we would get the original room card. However, when I called later, no one came to pick up the room card.
Also, even if all room fees and deposits are paid in advance, you still need to go to the front desk to swipe your card every day, otherwise the door will not open.
The location of the hotel is relatively remote. Choosing our hotel is entirely based on the filter of Nanjing Jinling Hotel. The actual check-in experience is not good. Ms. Liang at the front desk strictly abides by the hotel regulations, but she is also dogmatic and rigid. Not to mention the humanized service, at least for you With limited authority, even if you communicate with your supervisor...

msg:金源摩天輪單項體驗券:沒有被告知有這一項目
服務：很差的體驗。
           1.隔壁樓棟有KTV，入住時沒有告知，白天時就一直有聲音，以為是周邊廣場舞或者別的什麼，結果一直持續到晚上還在唱，問了前台才知道有KTV，除了換房間沒有別的處理方法，太麻煩了衹能硬忍到10點多才安靜下來。
           2.早餐廳快到收餐時間，酒店直接關空調，大概9點左右餐廳裏越來越熱，有別桌客人也都在説吃個早飯像蒸桑拿，問了餐廳服務員才知道每天這個時間空調都會關閉，服務員説因為快到收餐時間了。所以我可以理解為這是趕客操作嗎？？金陵飯店你這麼怕客人吃飯費電的話，就不要再做餐飲了。快捷酒店都沒有你們這種操作，頂着金陵的牌子，用這樣的模式經營，不噁心人嗎？

msg:特別失望的一次居住，充分暴露了金陵來到小縣城，酒店管理的不足自己服務意識的缺失。住店客人要停車，保安以地下車位沒有車位為由一概不讓停，讓客人隨便開到哪裡去找車位，事實是地下有很多空車位，也第一時間跟酒店取得聯繫告知希望能停車，然而酒店衹會説一句我們知道了，不會再理會你。另外就是由於有小孩，房間空調開着乾燥，於是電話前台問是否有加濕器可以借用，前台直接回覆沒有，因為朋友透露過他入住時是可以借的，於是跑到前台問是否可以借用，此時直接説可以的，也許換了一個人，就是不一樣的結果吧。另外就是電梯客梯時常有香煙味，房間地毯沒用吸塵器吸吧，我們入住的時候小朋友赤腳走路，腳上佔有毛髮，總之特別失望就是了，反饋了問題，沒任何人會給你反饋或者處理
🔔服務：沒有
🧹衞生：表面還行，不要赤腳走路
🚗 交通：保安很強勢，直接讓你別停進去，哪怕地下很多空車位（第一時間跟酒店溝通，還是不讓你停）理由是車位滿了，真心服了
